Shanghai-Guangdong Route Reopens 142

Guangdong Authorities Have Agreed Not to Obstruct

Yushun Arrives in Shantou: The Yushun ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company went to Hong Kong and Guangdong this time. It first went to Hong Kong, transported a large batch of sugarcane, and then went to Guangdong Province. When the ship arrived at the Qingshan Head sea area, it saw no way forward. The captain quickly ordered the ship to reverse and retreat to another route, but the ship's hull had already run aground in the shallows. At that time, there was no way to get out of danger, so they had to telegram Hong Kong for help. The Hong Kong authorities sent a barge to unload part of the cargo to reduce the weight and drag the ship out. Upon arriving in Guangdong, they were assigned to Shantou. Yesterday, a telegram was sent from Shanghai to Shantou to ask if it was possible to return to Shanghai, but no reply has been received yet.

Yuan'an Stays in Xiamen: The Yuan'an ship, which can be used in place of the Xinchang ship for Hong Kong and Guangdong routes, is making its first voyage south. It was originally intended to go directly to Guangzhou, but for the sake of caution and to avoid delaying the schedule, it went to Xiamen first and stayed there. The Guangzhou passengers and cargo on board were originally intended to be transshipped to Hong Kong, but since goods shipped from Hong Kong to Guangdong had to be taxed as foreign goods, they were transshipped in Xiamen and transported to Guangzhou by smaller ships, while Yuan'an stayed in Xiamen awaiting instructions.

Dispatching Personnel for Consultation: The Hong Kong branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has been停班 for another ten days since the Shanghai-Guangdong route was seized by the Party's货. A large number of goods and passengers are transported by foreign ships instead, which is like驱雀丛 and causes huge losses to Chinese merchants. The director of the Hong Kong branch personally went to Guangdong Province to request the provincial authorities not to detain ships in order to facilitate transportation and maintain shipping. After repeated discussions, the provincial authorities agreed to allow Chinese ships to go to Guangzhou without being detained or assigned officials.

Dispatching Ships to Guangdong: The Guangdong authorities have agreed not to detain merchant ships anymore, so the Hong Kong branch telegraphed Xiamen, ordering the Yuan'an ship to set sail for Guangzhou immediately and operate as usual. They also telegraphed Shanghai, reporting that the commissioner of the Hong Kong branch had agreed with the provincial authorities that ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company could operate as usual to Guangdong without obstruction and requesting that ships be dispatched quickly to resume the Shanghai-Guangdong service. Yesterday, the Shanghai branch received this telegram and has been planning to resume the Shanghai-Hong Kong-Guangdong service, which has been suspended. It also notified the Guangdong帮 that goods and passengers to Guangdong can be transported as usual from today. Once the Taishun ship returns to Shanghai and the Guangda ship leaves the dock, the service will be resumed immediately.

Motivation for China to Convene an International Silver Conference 145

Telegrams from Representatives Li and Bei

Mr. Chen Guangfu received telegrams yesterday from Li Guochin and Bei Songsun, our country's representatives attending the International Chamber of Commerce, stating: "President Chen Guangfu: According to your instructions, the representatives submitted the following proposal to the International Chamber of Commerce on May : 'The international economy is seriously affected by the current silver market. The International Chamber of Commerce should convene an international silver conference within this year to solve this urgent problem and urge the national chambers of commerce to ask their respective governments to pay attention to this.'" This proposal was passed by the delegates at the General Assembly on May 7 and has been submitted to the Proposals Committee for examination and implementation. As for the issue of silver and the global economic downturn, the representatives distributed more than 1,000 copies of the declaration, which resulted in a good phenomenon and deep interest. British government officials have made profound statements, expressing their willingness to formally join the conference and provide concrete cooperation. Arthur Balfour, the chief British representative, advocated that the conference should be held in the East, preferably in our country, and said that the British government would definitely join and support it. The Indian representative also enthusiastically supported this proposal. The Japanese representative also expressed his goodwill. The representative Nagami said that the method of saving silver prices should be drafted by our country, and Japan is very willing to cooperate when the conference is convened. According to the above-mentioned situation, the representatives believe that the present is an excellent opportunity for our country to convene an international silver conference. If the conference is organized perfectly, it will gain the participation of various countries and achieve success. We pray to the National Government to petition for its implementation as soon as possible. In this important event, please do not lose the opportunity to be an international leader because of domestic affairs. Please consider this carefully. Li Guochin, Bei Zuyi, respectfully." It is said that the China branch of the International Chamber of Commerce has already telegraphed the government for approval yesterday.

Special Aviation News 146

Japanese Fishing Boat Missing: Japanese fishing boats have come to our country to fish again after our country's ban was postponed. Recently, the Dalian Japanese Tanaka fishing boats Wan Yi Wan No. 5 and No. 6 went to Haizhou in our country to fish. No. 5 has been fully loaded with fresh fish and went to Qingdao for sale, while the whereabouts of No. 6 are unknown. It has been many days and it has not returned. The Japanese believe that they encountered theft in Haizhou. There are ten Japanese people on board. The owner of the fishing boat has specifically reported to the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai and requested that Japanese warships be sent to Qingdao and Haizhou to investigate.

Taiyin Ship Export: The Taiyin ship of the Tianxiang Shipping Company, one of the Pacific express ships, can reach New York in 36 days. It is scheduled to export from Shanghai on the 22nd and will be the first ship to New York after the new rules are issued by the Public Association. It will give special preferential treatment to export cargo.

City Health Movement Week to be Held Tomorrow 148

From the 15th to the 21st

The seventh Shanghai City Health Movement Week will be held from tomorrow (the 15th) to the 21st. A summary of the various activities to be held during the Movement Week is as follows: Large and small slogans: During this week (the seventh) of the Shanghai City Health Movement Week, the Municipal Health Bureau will produce and print a large number of slogans for publicity, so that citizens know the way to prevent cholera and pay attention to preventive measures. The large and small slogans printed by the bureau will be posted today (the 14th), with 40,000 stickers on rickshaws and military vehicles in the city, and 50,000 small and medium-sized slogans posted on walls along thoroughfares and in streetcars, buses, long-distance buses, and workshops. More than 70 health slogan boards will be hung in important locations in the city. In addition, the four existing advertising boards at the Baoshan Road intersection in the north of the city, the middle section of North Sichuan Road, the Xinzhapu bridgehead, and the Hengfeng Road bridgehead, as well as the four advertising boards in Nanshi, Xieqiao, Dadongmen, Dananmen, and Wusong Railway Station, have recently been repainted, depicting health slogans and color pictures of the dangers of cholera, making passersby aware of the coming summer, paying attention to hygiene, and preventing epidemics.

Street Sweeping: Tomorrow is the first day of the publicity week.

The Public Security Bureau will conduct a major street sweeping. The bureau will urge sanitation workers to carry out a special major sweeping on important roads in the urban area. Exempt from Parades: The Municipal Health Bureau believes that this Health

Movement Week falls during the busy month of May, so it will not hold parades and lectures in various districts as in previous years.

Free Injections: During the publicity week, citizens can

go to the Municipal Health Bureau in Maojia Lane, Nanshi, for cholera vaccinations. Doctors and hospitals entrusted by the bureau can provide free injections. Groups, organizations, companies, and firms with 30 people

Page 14

or more can notify the bureau in advance, and doctors will be sent directly to administer the injections free of charge.

Message to the Public: Hu Hongji, Director of the Health Bureau, yesterday issued a

message to the citizens for the seventh Health Movement, the original text is quite long, earnestly admonishing and encouraging people regarding the methods of summer hygiene and the dos and don'ts of diet and daily life.

Industry Association, Flower Industry Association, Noodle Skin Industry Association, Miscellaneous Grains Industry Association, Sesame Oil Industry Association, Lacquer Industry Association, Shaoxing Association, Chicken and Duck Industry Association, Sofa Number Industry Association, Cured Meat Industry Association, Blacksmith Industry Association, Native Cloth Industry Association, Construction Biscuit Dried Fruit Candy Canning Case, Silk Satin Industry Association, Chinese Medicine Industry Association, Electric Machine Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association, etc. The telegram reads as follows: "To Mr. Wang Yansong, Representative of the National Assembly Secretariat, Nanjing: Our country is suffering from the heavy shackles and layers of oppression of unequal treaties imposed by imperialists, and internally plagued by the rebellion of warlords who harm the country and the people. The people are haggard, and the country is about to perish. Colleagues who have experienced internal and external troubles have suffered the most. Therefore, businessmen's desire for governance is even greater than that of all sectors. Fortunately, with the efforts and struggles of our party comrades, the country has been unified, and the National Assembly has been opened as desired in accordance with the Prime Minister's will. Businessmen from all walks of life, in view of the depth of their suffering, have greater expectations for the National Assembly than other sectors. The responsibility of the businessmen's representatives is also becoming heavier. Shanghai is a gathering place for commerce, and the whole country's businessmen are watching. Mr. Representative of the Shanghai business community attending the National Assembly, your responsibility is even heavier. Now reading the newspaper, your proposal is that during the period of political tutelage, efforts should be made to restore national rights externally and to properly plan for the people's livelihood internally, which shows a clear understanding of the crux of the matter. All the public industry associations, in addition to sincerely supporting you, hope that you will persevere in striving to achieve the goal. We look forward to hearing from you soon." The original text of Wang's proposal is recorded as follows: "Since the government launched the Northern Expedition in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Hebei has been pacified two years later, and the whole country has entered the political tutelage program. However, rebellions have occurred repeatedly, and it has taken more than one attempt to quell them by force. In practice, it cannot be said that it has completely broken away from the era of military government. Therefore, the planned political tutelage facilities are inevitably clumsy. It was not until the end of the nineteenth year that the reactionary forces were gradually eliminated, and all facilities related to political tutelage could gradually be started. This time, the government is following the legacy of the teaching and convening the National Assembly to complete an important page of its political tutelage work. The main purpose of the National Assembly is to make the public have a deep understanding of the party platform of the Kuomintang, sincerely accept it, and at the same time, the public should select those that are suitable for the needs of the political tutelage period within the scope of the accepted party platform, and ask the government to implement them separately. This is actually the preliminary practice of the public's movement of political power. Considering the current situation, the public's needs in today's politics are to seek territorial integrity and sovereignty externally in order to restore national independence and national freedom. Internally, we must ensure that the 400 million people, although they cannot immediately reach the realm of adequate household income, can each maintain their minimum living standards, so that they have land to farm and industries to operate, and will not be displaced by disasters or take risks. This is indeed the most important task of the government today. In accordance with this idea, the following articles are proposed: (A) Those that belong to external affairs, such as the completion of tariff autonomy, have now come to an end. The abolition of consular jurisdiction is being actively pursued by the government, so there is no need to repeat it. In addition, it is believed that the government should devote all its efforts to the following matters in the next few years: (1) To recover the concessions, such as the Belgian concession in Tianjin and the British concession in Zhenjiang, which the countries concerned consider to be of little importance, but it still took considerable efforts from the diplomatic authorities to complete. As for the Japanese and French concessions in Hankou, which are relatively important, our country has been proposing them for several months, but the result is still delayed. Therefore, the recovery of the concessions, in terms of the past situation, is most difficult to proceed. The government should make double efforts. (2) To recover the leased territories and railway affiliated lands. Among the leased territories, such as France's Guangzhou Bay, there was an agreement to return it early in the Chinese Huai Conference, but now it is waiting and hesitant and unwilling to fulfill it, especially because the land is there, and it cannot be publicly overturned. Japan's lease of Lushun and Dalian Bay continues the Russian lease right, which was due early. As for the lease period extended according to Article 21, the matter was coerced, and our country's officials and people have long declared their denial. These two ports, one in the south and one in the north, are both important national defense areas of our country, and it is difficult to allow them to be occupied for a long time. As for the railway affiliated land, there is no clear provision in the unequal treaties. According to Article 16 of the Sino-Russian Agreement in Harbin in the first year of Xuantong, the so-called "land within the railway boundary that is exclusively for railway use, such as stations and factories, etc., may be managed by the company itself. The remaining land that has not been leased and the houses exclusively for the company's own use, according to the agreed drawings, not subject to the public council, will still be managed by the company itself temporarily. This remaining land should be temporarily exempted from land tax, etc." The nature of the so-called railway affiliated land is only that the railway company can manage its own land that has not been leased and is exempt from land rent. The South Manchurian Railway occupied by the Japanese can inherit a part of the Central Soviet Railway, and its rights cannot exceed those of the Central Eastern Railway. However, the Japanese hold the sole administrative power in the area, set up police and taxes, and regard it as an extension of the leased territory. Our country has been saying that it will abolish unequal treaties. The railway affiliated land is an unauthorized occupation beyond the unequal treaties and should be dealt with first in accordance with the treaty in order to seek the integrity of territorial rights. (3) To withdraw foreign troops stationed in the country. The stationing of these troops is based on unequal treaties. From Yuguan to Beiping, the origin is the Xin Chou Treaty, which is used to protect the transportation of its embassy from the capital to the sea. Now the situation has changed, and the mutual stationing of troops from various countries is either to maintain the balance of power or to have other intentions. It is not set up to protect the embassy's transportation and should have been negotiated and withdrawn long ago. As for those that exceed the unequal treaties, the situation of the South Manchurian Railway Garrison stationed by Japan is the most obvious. According to Article 2 of the Sino-Japanese Agreement on the Three Eastern Provinces in the thirty-first year of Guangxu, "The Government of Japan is willing to fulfill China's expectations, such as Russia agrees to withdraw its guard troops, or China and Russia have another well-negotiated method, the Government of Japan agrees to follow the same method." Russia withdrew its guard troops on the Central Eastern Road in the winter of the sixth year of the Republic of China. According to the agreement, Japan had no right to set up a garrison on the South Manchurian Road after the seventh year of the Republic of China. However, our country is accustomed to forgetting it, and Japan also regards the treaty as waste paper. This cannot but be attributed to the previous warlord government's playing and leaking to mislead the country. It is difficult to delay the situation any longer. (4) To negotiate with Russia and England to recover the sovereignty of Mongolia and Tibet. Since the Red Russia invaded Outer Mongolia, not only in the economic aspect, it has been manipulated by the abdomen, but also in the political and ideological aspects, it has been assimilated and anesthetized, no less than a dependency. According to the descriptions from various parties, not only has Tangnu Ulianghai been turned into territory long ago, but also many of the old place names of the four Khalkha tribes have been changed. Although Article 5 of the Sino-Russian Agreement has the condition of waiting for the Mongolian withdrawal, it is stated in Article 2 of this agreement that after negotiation in the meeting, the Soviet troops will be withdrawn from Mongolia in full. However, today the trouble of the Outer Mongolian heart and abdomen is no longer in the small number of Soviet troops stationed there, but in the all-encompassing political power. The remedy is to organize a party branch there by the central government, so that its politics can be carried out under the guidance of the party, and there is no way to get rid of the anesthesia of Red Russia. However, Outer Mongolia cannot receive merchants for transportation in one day, and it is still obstructed, let alone the transplant of party governance. Therefore, this Sino-Russian Moscow Conference must resolve the issue of receiving Outer Mongolia at the same time at the conference table, otherwise it will only discuss the restoration of trade and diplomacy, and I have not seen its benefits in practice, and the power of Red Russia is advancing southward from Outer Mongolia, and Inner Mongolia will also be affected by it. This is especially related to the national defense and safety of the provinces of Hebei and Shanxi and cannot be regarded as a slow plan. England's support for Tibet is no less deep than Russia's Outer Mongolia, or even more so. Since the collapse of the Sino-British Simla Conference, there is no agreement to restrain it, and England has continued its consistent policy in Tibet for more than ten years, and it is not as good as Russia's overthrow of the imperial system, its power in Outer Mongolia once faltered. Therefore, Outer Mongolian power has not publicly invaded Inner Mongolia, while England has used Tibet as a tiger to swallow almost three-quarters of the entire province of Xikang, and now it is advancing to Batang and Litang. In terms of border defense hidden dangers, it is more severe than Russia in Outer Mongolia. It should be proposed to negotiate with England together. In addition to acknowledging its historical trade relations in Tibet, all other political actions of our side, as the sovereign state, will be revoked, and it will be declared internally that there is no intention to assist the Dalai Lama in resisting China, so that Tibetan sovereignty may be recovered. (B) For internal affairs, the top priority should be to properly plan for the people's livelihood, as mentioned above. However, in terms of clothing, food, housing, and transportation, the old saying goes, "Food is the people's heaven," which seems to be particularly important. Moreover, the majority of our country's people are engaged in agriculture. If we can develop agriculture to solve the people's food problem, then purchasing power will increase, and the industrial and commercial sectors will also prosper, and clothing, housing, and transportation will also be solved in conjunction. Therefore, the government's current policy seems to be to focus on this with all the manpower and material resources that can be concentrated, in order to provide a key point. The matters that should be handled are briefly listed below: (1) The central government and the provincial governments should raise funds to organize large-scale immigration companies, lend agricultural tools, seeds, and build houses, and continue to immigrate to Xinjiang, Qinghai, Xikang, Chahar, and other places for a period of several years. After the expiration of the period, the atmosphere will be opened, and free immigrants will become more and more prosperous, then this move can be stopped. This will not only solve the unemployment problem and the rice shortage problem, but also consolidate the northwest border defense. (2) Disaster prevention fund. The government has had this plan, but it is impossible to speculate whether it is currently being implemented. It is believed that it should be strictly implemented according to the planned plan. If the annual budget is insufficient and the allocated funds cannot be equal to the amount, it seems appropriate to add some from the consumption tax on cigarettes to supplement it. After this fund is raised, some will be used to purchase food for storage and standby, roughly like the old system of storing grain, and some will be used exclusively for river management and forest cultivation in various provinces. The government's current financial resources are used to divert the Huai River and manage the Yellow River, all of which are used to withdraw the Gengzi indemnity, and there are many main rivers and tributaries in various provinces that are related to farmland rights and should be dredged. Since we must plan and take care of both, it is definitely necessary to open up another source of wealth, so as not to cause delay. (3) The improvement of agricultural crops and animal husbandry should be set as the performance evaluation of each county. The provincial government or the central government should select people with rich knowledge and technology to go to each county to guide and handle the matter, and the county government should be responsible for raising funds. This matter does not cost much. Ding County, Hebei, has already made some progress in recent years. It is said that if it is promoted year by year and continued for ten years, Ding County alone can increase production by 70 million yuan per year. This is a near path to solving the people's livelihood problem, but if the government does not preside over it, it will only be difficult for private forces to popularize it in the country. (4) To strictly limit the establishment of national farmers' banks. The reason why the rural economy cannot develop is entirely due to the lack of a low-interest financing agency. The farmers' bank is set up to remedy this defect. However, considering that those who have actually complied with the order to establish it, except for Jiangsu and Zhejiang, are rarely heard of. Moreover, although Jiangsu and Zhejiang have established them, they have not actually been popularized in each county, and there is little benefit to farmers. It is believed that the government should investigate the established ones to see if their achievements meet the needs of farmers, and those that have not been established should be strictly ordered to raise funds within a time limit. The government uses this as the performance evaluation of the provincial government, and the provincial government uses this as the performance evaluation of the county government, so that it will not be a day-to-day affair and there will be no deadline for completion. To sum up, the main points of working hard to restore national rights externally are: (1) To recover the concessions, (2) To recover the leased territories and railway affiliated lands, (3) To withdraw foreign troops stationed in the country, (4) To recover the sovereignty of Mongolia and Tibet. For internal affairs, the people's livelihood should be cultivated, starting with revitalizing farmland water conservancy. The main points are: (1) Immigration and reclamation, (2) Establishment of disaster prevention fund, (3) Improvement of agricultural work, (4) Universal establishment of farmers' banks, all of which are considered in the order of priority and the current financial resources of the government. I dare not make any exaggerated remarks to avoid any blame. As for the articles on properly planning for the people's livelihood, it seems appropriate to stipulate them in the chapter on national economic law, so that officials and people can share their faith and abide by them. Is there any correctness in submitting it for public decision?

Jiangsu Meat Industry Holds Trade Association Congress Yesterday 154

Opposing the Collection of Slaughter Tax

The Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association, due to the municipal government's point-by-point collection of slaughter tax, has aroused unanimous opposition from the industry throughout the city. Pacific and New York Line Far East Shipping Alliance 156

Resisting the Disruption of Non-Member Ships

Establishing New Rules for Pre-arranged Contracts

This year, the competition between Sino-American shipping lines is the most intense and the turmoil is the greatest. On the Pacific and New York routes, new ships are being launched at fast speeds. Generally, ships that are not members of the alliance are drastically lowering freight rates, causing indescribable chaos. Therefore, almost all Sino-American liners are suffering losses. Now, the shipping freight alliance has specially convened all members to discuss relief measures in order to resist the disruption of non-member ships. They have agreed on new methods to resist non-member ships, to be implemented on the 15th. This matter is of utmost importance to the shipping industry, and a detailed account of the situation is recorded as follows:

General Meeting The Freight Alliance Operating on the New York Route

To unite the strength of its members due to the increasing number of non-member ships, and to jointly fight against non-member ships in unison with the Pacific Shipping Alliance, this time all members were convened. Representatives from eighteen shipping companies attended, including American-Mongolian Shipping Company Baohe Agency, Babb Shipping Company, Tianxiang Manager, Blue Funnel Company Battery Company, Tianxiang Agency Dalaiyang Firm, Nippon Yusen Kaisha, Osaka Company, American Post Changxing, Jardine Matheson, and Kawasaki. They agreed on a new freight rate, divided into a pre-arranged contract rate for members' ships and a non-contract rate, so that cargo can be attracted, and disruptors will have no way to apply their tricks.

New Rate Types After discussion, the alliance stipulated new

rules, the method is, for all export goods loaded to the Pacific or New York routes, there has always been only one freight rate. Now, it is divided into two: (1) For customers who load on ships of alliance members and who sign a shipping contract in advance, the freight rate can enjoy special benefits. Regardless of the type of goods, the freight can be reduced by two US dollars per ton (approximately eight yuan in Shanghai currency). (2) If customers do not sign a loading contract with members in advance, the freight rate will be cancelled according to the newly established rate, which is two US dollars more expensive compared to signing a contract. It is stipulated that customers who sign contracts this month must not load non-member ships starting on the 15th.

Freight Contents After a detailed investigation by the reporter, the contents of the two types of freight are specially recorded as follows:

(Goods Name) (Quantity) (Contract Price) (Non-Contract Price) Ore Per Ton Six Dollars and Fifty Cents Eight Dollars and Fifty Cents

Duck Feathers Per Ton 10.0 22.0

Oils Per Ton 6.5 85.

Eggs Per Ton 10.0 12.0

Tobacco Leaves Per Ton 12.0 14.0

Copperware Per Ton 14.0 16.0

Leather Per Ton Six Dollars and Fifty Cents Eight Dollars and Fifty Cents

Walnuts Per Ton 6.5 8.5

Tea Leaves Per Ton 8.5 10.5

Ramie Per Ton 7.5 9.5

Wool Per Ton 8.0 10.0

Miscellaneous Goods Per Ton 14.0 16.0

Signing Contracts Competitively After the announcement of this new method, major foreign firms in Shanghai handling export business, such as Yuntong, Anding, Beide, Flander, Ruifeng, Longmao, Shunyu, and Jardine Matheson, all went to the alliance yesterday to request signing pre-arranged contracts for loading Pacific and New York export goods in order to enjoy superior freight benefits. Yesterday, twelve firms reported signing contracts. It is expected that the number of attendees signing this loading contract will increase even more in the next two days.

Requesting Membership The new rules of the two alliances this time are enough to determine the fate of the general disruptive wildcat ships that have not joined the alliance. Where there is profit, people will inevitably flock to it. American firm Fulaiyang, which also newly operates the Pacific-New York route, has not yet joined the alliance. Upon receiving this news, its manager, Mr. Afolited, has reported requesting to join as a member. After a general meeting resolution, it is hoped that his membership will be approved. Those who have not joined the alliance will no longer be able to engage in irregular competition in the future.

Yesterday's News of the Bookbinding Industry Strike 157

The Social Affairs Bureau Ordered to Resume Work First

The Apprentice Problem Has Been Resolved

Eighty-five bookbinding workshops, including Ma Hongji, which does both Chinese and Western-style bookbinding, have been on strike in this city. Yesterday, fifty more shops, including Zhu Jinji, joined the strike, greatly affecting publications. The apprentice problem was resolved yesterday through mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau. The wage issue still needs to be reviewed and handled. It is also ordered to resume work immediately. The details of each situation are recorded separately below:

Strike Expanded The day before yesterday, more than 1,200 workers from eighty-five Chinese and Western-style bookbinding workshops, including Ma Hongji, in the Zhabei area, went on strike because their request to amend the terms of treatment and increase wages by 40% was not met. Yesterday, more than 500 workers from more than forty workshops, including Zhu Jinji, Pu Xieji, Shen Heji, Lu Guiji, and Tang Yunji, in the British Concession, more than one hundred workers from six workshops, including Wu Fuju and Shu Yiji, in the Nanshi, and more than two hundred workers from more than ten workshops, including Shen Ji, Chen Xieji, and Qin Bingji, in the Yangshupu area, uniformly joined the strike. As a result, the number of strikers has increased to more than 2,000, and there are already 240 workshops on strike. If this is extended, publications will inevitably be greatly affected.

Mediation Meeting Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau

convened labor and management for mediation. Ding Handong and Xu Hanqing, representatives from the bookbinding industry association, and Chen Zhaoqing and Ren Changfu, representatives from the bookbinding industry union, attended. The meeting was chaired by Yin Yongxi from the Social Affairs Bureau and recorded by Wang Huqin. The labor side stated the reasons for the workers' strike, saying that the management had no sincerity in accepting the conditions. The management stated the reasons for not being able to accept them. After a lengthy discussion, the chairman considered repeatedly and stated briefly that the bureau would order the workers to resume work immediately. Regarding the issue of wage increases, he ordered the management to turn to the book industry association to request it, and a firm reply must be given within ten days. Then, the bureau will convene mediation in accordance with the law.

Apprentice Problem In accordance with the city's interim apprentice rules

and factory standards for employing apprentices, ordinary workers, those with fewer than fifty workers, can recruit five apprentices, those with more than one hundred workers can recruit fifteen apprentices, and those with more than three hundred workers can recruit twenty apprentices. If there is an organizational branch, the number is based on each branch. Male and female children under the age of twelve must not be employed. The management representative agreed to comply with this. The labor representative agreed to find ways to persuade the workers to resume work on the 15th.

The Incense and Candle Industry Again Requests a Reduction in Business Tax 158

The City Candle Industry Association requested a reduction in the business tax on incense and candles. Yesterday, it sent a document to the various industry associations' tax rate research committee, stating that it was submitting a request for the Shanghai Municipal Government to reduce the business tax on incense and candles because the tax rate was too high. It should be listed as the same as the candle and soap industry. It said, "Having read in the newspaper that the Shanghai Municipal Government has now formulated a standard business tax rate table, with the item of incense and candles having a tax rate of 10 per mille, etc., after reading it, we were extremely alarmed. Upon investigation, both incense and candles are daily necessities. Now, the government taxes them at 10 per mille, which seems to be unevenly weighted compared to the candle and soap industry, which is of equal nature. The reviewing officials consider candles and soap to be daily necessities for the people, and taxing them too heavily may be detrimental to people's livelihoods. Therefore, they have carefully considered reducing it and levying a tax rate of 1 per mille, understanding the difficulties of merchants, which cannot be said to be not thorough. Now, for incense and candles, which have the same function, a tax ten times heavier is added. Favoring one over the other is probably not the original intention of the reviewing officials. Probably because there are many categories and the review is inevitably flawed, the industry feels left out. Now, we humbly present the reasons for the amendment and reduction that should be made, and we urge you to review and transfer them. According to the items of candles and soap, one is to replace the lamp, and the other is to remove dirt. The function is originally very grand and universal. However, the products of our industry, such as incense, are enough to kill insects and stop odor, and are prepared by households, which are not inferior to soap. As for native candles and foreign candles, the materials are the same, and the uses are exactly the same. The weight is the same. For tax rules, there should be no difference at all. Secondly, foreign candles are more expensive than native candles. In poor rural areas, due to financial constraints, those who abandon them and use them cannot be counted. Our government strives to keep the tax rate low for universally used items for the poor and hardship classes in order to relieve people's difficulties, and all the lands are covered. This is the second reason why the tax on native candles should not be increased. Our industry originally did not dare to complain about the government's measures. However, the facts are like this, so how can we remain silent? Therefore, we specially state the situation below, and we urge your association to quickly strive hard according to the facts, and be sure to revise the business tax rate of the incense and candle industry to 1 per mille in order to alleviate business difficulties and value people's livelihoods. We will be extremely grateful."

Flour Broker Pan Ruijie Was Almost Kidnapped 165

Fortunately, He Jumped Out of the Car to Escape

At 10:45 AM yesterday, a kidnapping case occurred at the entrance of the New Kaihe Flour Exchange in Nanshi. The details are recorded as follows:

Operating Flour Pan Jiachi, with the courtesy name Ruijie, is a broker

at No. 52 of the exchange. He is from Luodian and is 47 years old. He used to open the Ruiji Flour Company at the entrance of Gongyi Lane on New Laji Bridge, specializing in the spot flour of Fufeng Company. His residence is rented in a foreign house at No. 138 Papu Road in the French Concession.

Once Kidnapped After being kidnapped and ransomed once in

October of last year, his whereabouts were slightly secretive, but he still went to the exchange every day, riding a black car he prepared himself. The license plate number of the car is 3326 in the Public Concession and 2378 in the Chinese area. He went to the exchange to work, rain or shine.

Encountered Danger for the Second Time Unexpectedly, after the flour market

closed yesterday, Pan sent the doorman to call the car parked at the entrance of Danfeng Street to come over, preparing to board the car to go to the Ruiji Company to inspect matters. At that time, a young man in a Western suit asked Sun Yufeng, the gatekeeper of the exchange, whether the flour exchange was about to move. The gatekeeper did not take it seriously and nodded, saying yes, and also told him where to move.

Three Kidnappers At that time, Pan's chauffeur, Shi Jiajun, from

Yangzhou (24 years old), had already driven the car close to the entrance. Pan then called his son, Pan Fangkang, to get into the car first, and he followed. However, the left side of the car door was not closed. The chauffeur was about to turn the engine, when three people wearing black robes and standing in the French Concession, tall and mighty, rushed quickly to the car.

The Hostage Escaped Each of the three people held a handgun, first

scaring the chauffeur into silence and forcing him to get out of the car. One person held a gun and opened the right side of the car door, seemingly threatening. Although Pan was burly, he was very alert and knew they were not good people. So, he kicked open the left side of the car door with one foot, jumped down with a strong force, and ran into the head door of the exchange, shouting kidnapping.

Police Surrounded and Arrested At that time, the gatekeeper and

pedestrians on the street began to pay attention and shouted in unison. The four robbers, each holding a handgun, sped away in a car parked on the side of the road towards the French Concession. After the news was received by the second division of the first district, Chief Inspector Mao Shengzheng led the entire police team to surround and arrest them. However, they were nowhere to be found. They returned to the scene of the incident to investigate and strictly investigate, but according to Pan, he had not received a threatening letter beforehand.

Seeking Compensation for Losses from the Public Works Department

Someone Offered to Buy the Greyhounds

Three Children Were Burned to Death in a Careless Fire in a Caojiadu Shack 167

Two Other Children Were Burned

A Cry of Disaster Victims

At about 9:45 AM yesterday (the 13th), on the wasteland at the intersection of Binlang Road, opposite the Gongyi Yarn Factory on Labosheng Road in West Shanghai, a fire broke out in shack No. 10, where Jiangbei poor people lived. While cooking, they inadvertently left the fire unattended, and suddenly thick smoke filled the air and pierced the roof. The police officer on duty there saw it and immediately reported it to the Caojiadu Fire Brigade, which drove to the scene to put out the fire. However, because the shacks were close together and the wind was blowing violently, the fire had spread widely, and there was a blaze of fire. After the firefighters worked hard to put out the fire, it was extinguished after about an hour. It is estimated that 30 to 40 shacks were burned down. Because the fire was fierce, two boys and one girl were hiding in the fire pit. Two other boys and one girl had their skin burned. The firefighters then dug out the bodies of the three children, all of whom had become charred wood, which was unbearable to witness. One body had its limbs burned off. After being identified by their families (one boy named Qiao Longkouzi, four years old, another boy named Xia Xiaokouzi, also four years old, and one girl named Feng Xiaomazi, also four years old, all from Gaoyou), they were taken back for burial. The two injured children were also sent to the hospital for treatment, and their injuries were quite severe. At that time, dozens of poor people, big and small, who were affected by the disaster, gathered at the fire scene, wailing and crying, which was extremely miserable. Then, Chief Ren, the district chief of the sixth district police station, sent police to the scene to investigate for a week, and immediately detained Wang Xueshi (28 years old), a woman from Baoying who was in charge of the fire, and brought her back to the station for interrogation. After an interrogation, she immediately prepared a document and sent it to the third section of the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

An 18-Year-Old Apprentice Blackmailed a Doctor 168

The Doctor Received a Total of Eight Letters

The Handwriting Seems to Be from Two People

A Letter After Zhu Genli Was Kidnapped

It Is Also Related to the Apprentice

On the 17th of last month, someone went to a doctor's clinic and asked him to go to Li Shengmin's house at No. 702 Hadong Road to treat a disease. The doctor went by car. When he arrived at his destination, he asked around and found no one by the name of Li Min. So, he drove back. The next day, he received a letter delivered by mail, signed by Li Shengmin, which stated that the invitation to the doctor yesterday was originally intended to kidnap him, but because of face, he was not harmed. Please send 55,000 yuan to Xibaoshan Road, Zhabei, as soon as possible. The letter included a bullet. The doctor sent someone to the agreed place to negotiate, but no one arrived after waiting for a long time, so he gave up. However, he received as many as four threatening letters after this. On the 3rd of this month, he received a letter signed by the San Kai Party, demanding 1,000 yuan and instructing him to send the money to Gan Weimin at No. 2 Beifujian Road Printing Office. The doctor reported the information, and the police wrote a reply. The day before yesterday, Gan's reply was received, and Detective Wang Yingjie was sent to disguise himself and wait in front of the printing office. At the same time, a letter in Gan's name was sent by the postman. He saw Huang Yongqing, an 18-year-old worker from Wuxi, receiving the letter. Detective Wang arrested him without waiting for him to open it. He then went to Huang's house at No. 733 Maigen Road and found the reply to Gan Weimin's letter. Only then did he know that Gan was Huang's pseudonym. However, the handwriting of the letters signed by the San Kai Party and Gan was different from that of the letters signed by Li Shengmin. Therefore, it is not yet possible to determine whether the eight letters before and after were written by the same bandit. However, according to the police's identification, the handwriting of the last two letters was similar to that of the threatening letters received after Zhu Genli, who lived at No. 212 Changsha Road, was kidnapped. Therefore, it is speculated that Huang Yongqing may be related to the kidnapping and blackmail of Zhu. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Special District Local Court for questioning. The defendant hired a lawyer to defend him, saying that the defendant was only 16 years old. When asked about it, Huang admitted that the last two letters were written by him. Judge Xu Ting ordered him to be detained for further questioning because the police still needed to investigate.

The Widow of Shen Xuan Fell into the River

The No. 876 Sampan Escaped

Yesterday, the Weituoma Road Water Police Station received a phone call from the Blue Funnel Wharf reporting that a female corpse had floated up. The sampan was seized, but the boatman had escaped. However, it was in the middle of the night, so it was very confusing as to why the deceased crossed the river and died in Pudong. But the boatman escaped, so it is difficult to find the truth. Her body has been taken to the Southern Wharf Life Saving Bureau. It has now been reported to the Local Court for inspection.

Someone Was Sleeping on the Bed When He Returned Home in the Middle of the Night 170

Wang Weihu Was Naturally Furious

Fu Liu's Head Was Cut with a Knife

The Assault Resulted from a Reason

Sentenced to Three Months in Prison with a Two-Year Reprieve

Wang Weicai from Suqian and his wife, Xie, had lived at No. 107 Xiamen Road for a long time. Fu Liu lived at No. 99 next door and often went to Wang's house to chat. Because Xie was slightly beautiful, he often teased her. It was not until July of last year that they had a relationship. From then on, they secretly cheated, and Wang did not know. On the evening of the 10th of this month, Fu Liu learned that Wang had gone out, sneaked into Xie's inner room, and indulged in love. At midnight, Wang returned, and Fu was still sleeping with the woman. Wang was filled with anger when he saw this dirty sight. He ran to the kitchen and took a sharp knife to the room to commit violence. Although Fu was aware of it, he did not have time to escape. His head was cut with a knife. Wang wanted to commit suicide, but the second landlord arrived and persuaded him. Wang threw the knife on the ground and accidentally injured his foot. Fu took the opportunity to escape. The next morning, Wang surrendered to the Laoza Police Station, saying that he had been harmed by Fu for no reason. The head of the police sent detectives to arrest Fu, but he was nowhere to be found. So, he sent Wang to the hospital for treatment. On the way, he told the detectives the reason for the quarrel. The detectives believed that Wang should not have made false accusations, so they brought him back to the police station and waited for investigation. The night before last, the police detectives were performing inspection duties on the tram on Beihai Road. They saw a passenger with a head injury. When asked, he said he was Fu Liu. So, they took him to the police station. The head of the police questioned why he did not report it at the time. Fu replied that he knew he was wrong. The head of the police ordered the detectives to summon Xie to the police station for questioning. According to her, Fu often came to her room with a sharp blade. Because she was afraid of his power, she endured the humiliation and followed him, against her will. The head of the police waved her away and ordered her to go to the Special District Local Court for questioning the next morning. Yesterday morning, the Special Court interrogated her. Xie avoided appearing in court. After Judge Xu Ting interrogated Fu and Wang, he found that Wang Weicai had committed violence with a knife and injured someone. He sentenced him to three months in prison with a two-year reprieve, taking into account that the incident was caused by a reason. The knife was confiscated.

Scheduled Ferry Service Between Dinghai Bridge and Qingningsi Opens 172

Starts on the 16th of this month

One departure every ten minutes

The area between Dinghai Bridge in Puxi and Qingningsi in Pudong sees many workers from Qingningsi working in factories in Yangshupu, commuting early in the morning and late at night, making the traffic extremely frequent. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities once tried to operate a cross-river ferry service here in the 17th year of the Republic, but it was discontinued due to the shallow and silted shores on the Puxi side, which made it difficult for the ferry to dock. However, recognizing the need, the bureau included the cross-river ferry service in the first phase of its expansion plan when it considered expanding the municipal ferry service last year. Subsequently, it ordered the construction of ferries and, under the supervision of the Bureau of Public Works, built floating docks, actively preparing for the service. The ferry and the Qingningsi dock had already been inspected and accepted, and the Dinghai Bridge dock was recently completed. It is reported that the Bureau of Public Utilities has scheduled the official launch of the ferry service starting on the 16th of this month, with departures every ten minutes from 5:00 AM to 8:00 PM. The fare is eight copper coins per person per trip, and vehicles and goods can also be transported at a low cost. From now on, transportation on both sides of the Huangpu River will have another important hub.

Municipal Finance Bureau Extends the Exchange Period for Rent Voucher Tickets 173

Extended for another half month

Deadline is the 25th of this month

The exchange of rent voucher tickets in this city, which were requisitioned earlier, was started by the Municipal Finance Bureau on February 6th of this year, originally scheduled to end on March 6th. Later, with the approval of the Municipal Government, the bureau extended the period for one month, continuing the exchange from April 11th. This was announced in various newspapers and notices were posted to inform the public. Now, the extended period is about to expire again. After verification by the bureau, there are still a small number of vouchers that have not been exchanged. Article 2 of the Regulations for Exchanging Vouchers stipulates that exchanges are not allowed after the deadline. Moreover, the deadline could have been enforced after the extension. However, the Municipal Government, considering that some owners holding these vouchers may not have been able to come to the bureau to exchange them due to certain reasons, has approved the bureau's request to extend the period for another half month, starting from the 11th of this month, to protect their rights. It is said that after this extension, the deadline will be enforced according to the law.

Prohibition of Temple Fair in Jiangwan Town 174

District Chief Dai Issues a Public Notice

Dai Hongen, the chief of the Fifth Precinct and Fifth Sub-station of the Jiangwan Town Public Security Bureau, issued a public notice the day before yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of public notice, temple fairs and welcoming gods are superstitious activities and have been strictly prohibited by repeated orders from the Public Security Bureau. Recently, it has been heard that merchants and residents of this town, clinging to old habits, are still planning to hold a fair on the 28th day of the abolished lunar third month, which wastes money and time. Moreover, communist bandits are lurking in various places, constantly plotting disturbances, which may take advantage of the opportunity to disrupt public order, which is not insignificant. It is the duty of this office to plan ahead and prevent problems before they arise. Therefore, a public notice is hereby issued to prohibit such activities in order to prevent problems from arising. Anyone who deliberately violates this prohibition will be investigated and dealt with according to the law. This is the public notice."

Further Report on the Conflict Between Fishing Boats and the Shipping Department in Wusong Yunzaobang 176

Yesterday's newspaper reported on the misunderstanding that occurred between fishing boats docked in Wusong Yunzaobang and the Shipping Department of the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities, which led to a conflict. It is now learned that the fishermen were greatly angered after the incident, so they refused to unload any of their catch for sale. Yesterday, various fish markets showed signs of closing down, and various businesses were panicked. Details are described as follows:

Business Letter: Most of the commercial market in Wusong relies on the fishing season. After hearing this news, everyone panicked and held a temporary meeting. They jointly sent a letter to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce for assistance. The businesses that signed the letter included Gan Fengtai, Hua Chang, Wan Sheng, Rui Long, Fu Chang, Yong Feng, and more than 200 others.

Yesterday's Situation: Yesterday, the crew members of various fishing boats refused to work because the case of the Shipping Department of the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities injuring the crew members had not been resolved. Therefore, the fish in the cabins could not be unloaded for sale, and various fish markets were virtually closed, creating an atmosphere of panic. People flocked to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, waiting anxiously for a solution. Until about 4:00 PM, Yang Shaozhen, the director of the Shipping Department, replied to Zheng Shushan, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, saying that he had reported the situation to the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities and that he could not solve it. At that time, the water patrol team suddenly sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce, handing over Wang Jinyu, Lü Wanzhi, Lü Wannian, and Lü Wancheng, who had been bailed out the day before, saying that they were ordered by their superiors to transfer them to the court. However, the Bureau of Public Utilities did not send anyone to Wusong, so the Chamber of Commerce could not mediate.

Dispatching Personnel for Investigation: The Society Bureau paid close attention to this incident due to its impact on the Wusong market. Therefore, Wang Defa was sent to Wusong around 1:00 PM yesterday to investigate the incident with various institutions in Wusong and fish markets such as Cuisheng, Baofeng, and Shentai. He returned to Shanghai around 4:00 PM to report the situation for verification.

Crew Members File Lawsuit: Wang Jinyu, the injured crew member, was sent to the Haibin Public Hospital for treatment by the Chamber of Commerce the day before. Jiang Yisheng, the president of the hospital, and the doctor examined the injuries and signed a medical certificate, which stated: "Wang Jinyu, 39 years old, from Yancheng, Jiangsu, a sailor, was sent by the Wusong Chamber of Commerce. (Self-report) He was hit with a pole around 2:00 PM today, causing a lot of bleeding from his head and severe pain. (Diagnosis) The skin on the top of the head from front to back is torn, about 6 cm long and about 1 cm deep. There are subcutaneous hematomas on both sides of the back of the head, each about 5 cm long and about 4 cm wide. Signed on May 12th, the 20th year of the Republic of China, at 3:00 PM." After being arrested and released on bail, the four crew members Wang Jinyu, Lü Wanzhi, Lü Wannian, and Lü Wancheng, learned that Wang Guodong, the president of the Yancheng Chamber of Commerce, was in Wusong for business and was also very indignant. Therefore, he went to Shanghai yesterday to hire lawyer Zhu Dianqing to draft a lawsuit, which is scheduled to be filed with the Local Court tomorrow (the 14th), accusing Director Yang of the Shipping Department of a criminal offense.

Factories Emphasize Security 182

More than 40 factories, including Sanyou and Zhufeng, which are members of the Shanghai Machinery Industry Association, recently sent representatives to visit the Kangyuan Canning Factory on Huade Road. They requested a demonstration of emergency preparedness on the spot. The simulated fire was fierce. Upon hearing the alarm, the factory workers quickly gathered. In an instant, the rescue team rescued people and protected the doors, the transport team moved out important books and records, and the extinguishing team extinguished the fire with sand and water. The spreading fire was extinguished in an instant. With a whistle, the team returned to work. It took no more than two minutes to complete everything. Their agility and orderliness surpassed even well-trained soldiers. The representatives of various factories were full of praise and said that they would follow suit.

Mr. and Mrs. J. V. Crowe, the manager of the Ford Motor Company in Shanghai, are scheduled to return to the United States on the Tatsuta Maru of the Japan Mail Steamship Company on the 16th of this month. It is said that this trip to the United States is for negotiations with the Ford Motor Company's head office. Also departing for the United States are Mr. M. L. Wiesmyer and Mr. F. C. Riecks of the Ford Motor Company's head office in Detroit, Michigan.

Retrial of Young Woman's Lawsuit Demanding Alimony Opens 184

Judge Persuasively Tries to Reconcile

Young Woman Remains Uncompromising

The case of Xu Xishi, a young woman from Shanghai who filed a lawsuit against her father-in-law, Xu Zhilan, demanding alimony of 10,000 yuan because she refused to live with her husband, was appealed by Xu Zhilan. The retrial was held at the Jiangsu High Court the day before yesterday. As reported in yesterday's newspaper, the two parties involved in the case were an elderly man with white hair and a young woman with elegant demeanor, presenting an interesting contrast in court. The details of the interrogation on that day are recorded as follows: Around 3:00 PM, Zheng Zhiguo, the presiding judge, summoned Xu Zhilan to the deliberation chamber first. (Question) Has the family been divided? (Answer) The family was divided last month. (Question) Is your appeal because you are unwilling to pay alimony? (Answer) My business has been losing money in recent years, and I am heavily in debt. I really have no ability to pay such a large sum. (Question) Then how do you plan to deal with your daughter-in-law? (Answer) I want them to live together as husband and wife. My ancestral home is Ningbo, and I still have some thin fields that are enough to live a simple life. We should share blessings and misfortunes together. Demanding alimony is really impossible. Moreover, I am already over sixty years old and my energy is declining. According to regulations, I should be supported by my children, how can a father-in-law support his daughter-in-law? At this time, Fan Ming, the lawyer representing the appellee, submitted a list of Xu Zhilan's current assets, which stated that he had about 600,000 yuan in property. However, Xu Zhilan pointed out one by one that some properties had been mortgaged and some properties had been sold. After offsetting each other, he was still in debt. The judge then summoned Xu Ding's, (Question) What is your opinion on the original judgment? (Answer) In addition to alimony, I also need 8,000 yuan for my young daughter's education expenses. (Question) Do you know how much property your father-in-law has now? (Answer) About 100,000 yuan. (Question) Can you specify the various properties? Xu Ding's was silent and unable to answer. The judge then asked, "Have you and your husband always been harmonious?" (Answer) Very harmonious. (Question) Have you always lived together? (Answer) We lived together. The judge then summoned Xu Xiaofu to the court, (Question) Where do you live now? (Answer) I live with my brother now. (Question) Did you sign the separation agreement yourself? (Answer) Yes. (Question) Do you know how much property your father has? (Answer) There is no property now. (Question) Do you have a daughter? (Answer) Yes. (Question) Does your father treat you well? (Answer) They treat me well. (Question) Are you and your wife harmonious? (Answer) We have always been harmonious. However, since I suffered from madness last year, she often drove me out, did not give me clothes, and did not give me food. I had no choice but to live with my brother temporarily. (Question) Do you want to live with your wife now? (Answer) I really want to. I hope the judge will fulfill my wish. At this point, the judge tried to mediate, saying to both parties, "This case is a family misfortune. It is rare for a daughter-in-law to sue her father-in-law. I think it is better to reconcile." He then asked Xu Zhilan, "What is your intention?" (Answer) I have two options: (1) I will go home and live with my husband, and I will treat each room equally. (2) Or call her to live in Ningbo, because there are ancestral fields in Ningbo that can support her. The judge then asked Xu Ding's, "How about living with your husband?" (Answer) I don't want to. (Question) Since you are husband and wife, you should live together. It is better for you to go to Ningbo with your husband. (Answer) I am not used to living in Ningbo, and I am afraid of being bullied by them in Shanghai. (Question) Since you married a Ningbo man, you should go to Ningbo. Moreover, you are now demanding alimony, which may not necessarily be fulfilled. Even if you can achieve the goal of 10,000 yuan, how many years can you use it? In the future, it will still be useless. However, despite the judge's gentle persuasion, Xu Ding's remained stubborn, and the result was ineffective. Shen Yuan, the presiding judge of the First Civil Court, then changed to the First Court and ordered the two lawyers to begin the debate. First, Zhong Hongsheng, the lawyer for the original appellant, strongly argued that Xu Ding's demand for alimony had no legal basis and was unreasonable. He also cited the Family Law and asked the court to revoke the original judgment. Then, Zhang Henghai, the second lawyer for the original appellant, supplemented that the original appellant was factually unable to bear the alimony, and it should also be rejected in reason. Then, Fan Ming, the lawyer representing the appellee, responded, requesting that the original judgment be upheld. Around 5:00 PM, the judge declared the debate in this case to be concluded and announced that the judgment would be announced on the 15th of this month.

Fire at Dongjiadu Straw Paper Factory 185

The Lidachao Straw Paper Factory, opened by Yao Chunrong from Wuxi at the southern end of Sanguantang, Dongjiadu, Pudong, has been around for seven or eight years. Later, due to the prosperous business, a rope-making factory was added two years ago. Both factories employ seventy or eighty male and female workers. Yao and his wife closed the door yesterday morning and went to Puxi to visit their relatives. Unexpectedly, at 3:30 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in the pile of rice straw at the door of the factory. Thick smoke filled the air, and then the fire broke out. At that time, the wind was quite strong, and the fire quickly spread, making it impossible to approach. The workers fled outwards. The police officers from the Third Sub-precinct and Third Precinct reported to the precinct, and Director Dong immediately led all the police officers to the scene and sounded the alarm whistle. Soon, the Huachang Kenpian Factory and the Dongjiadu Special Zone Fire Brigade in Puxi drove water pump trucks to the scene one after another and tried their best to put out the fire. By 5:00 PM in the evening, the fire gradually subsided and was extinguished. In total, more than ten thatched houses, tens of thousands of bundles of rice straw, and more than sixty rope-making machines (each worth about thirty yuan) were burned down. In addition, Yao's furniture, clothing, and miscellaneous items in his bedroom were also greatly damaged. It is said that the fire was caused by a careless worker throwing a cigarette butt into the pile of straw, causing the fire.

Minutes of the Board Meeting of the American Eastern Bank 186

At the board meeting of the American Eastern Bank on the 8th of this month, it was resolved to hold a special shareholders' meeting at the office at 29 Nanjing Road at 5:00 PM on the 18th of this month to propose an amendment to the company's articles of association. The proposal is to split each share of preferred stock and Class A common stock into five shares. The par value was originally 100 yuan in Shanghai general currency. Now, by dividing into five shares, each share will be worth 20 yuan, which is the same as the par value of Class B common stock, in order to unify the price and facilitate trading on the market. According to the recent market price of Class A common stock, which is 135 yuan, all 25,485 shares of Class A common stock and 77 shares of preferred stock will be split into smaller shares after this proposal is passed. The proposal can be implemented with the approval of two-thirds of the shareholders.

Review of Rent Reduction Movement by Tenants in Chengzhi Lane 187

Wanlong Sauce Garden, Tianjitang, and five other households in Chengzhi Lane (formerly Fuxing Lane) on Moulin Street in the French Concession hired lawyer Zheng Yuxiu to sue the landlord Xia Guifang in the French Public Concession for demanding rent reduction. The court ruled to dismiss the case. The plaintiffs were dissatisfied and hired lawyer Yao Zhaodi to represent them and request a review. Yesterday, after being summoned, the lawyer representing the plaintiffs first stated that the court had not thoroughly investigated the case during the initial trial and dismissed the case, so they requested a review. Now there are four requests: (1) Reduce the rent by 30%. (2) Recover the small rent. (3) Reduce one month's rent. (4) Do not increase the rent within five years. Regarding the rent reduction, the defendant's rent is more expensive than the rent in the neighboring areas. According to the regulations for suppressing rent issued by the former Consul General Wei in Shanghai and Article 442 of the Civil Code on housing regulations, they are all contrary. As for the small rent, the plaintiffs each paid six or seven months' small rent when they moved in, which is considerable, so they requested to recover it. Moreover, the house was completed at the end of September, but the landlord actually published a notice requiring all tenants to pay rent starting from September, which is unreasonable. It is found that the land at that location covers a total of three mu, six fen, and eight li. According to the municipal price of the Engineering Bureau, each mu is no more than 35,000 taels, totaling more than 100,000 taels. The construction cost of the house is found to be made of old materials, which did not cost much. Calculating the defendant's cost, the agreed rent is too high. The court should revoke the initial trial's ruling and approve the plaintiffs' request. The defendant Xia Guifang was represented by lawyer Peng Qi, who argued that, to rent a house, one must agree to the landlord's contract terms, otherwise there is no argument to be made. When the plaintiffs rented the house from the landlord, the rent amount was agreed upon in advance, so how can they renege afterwards? As for how much the landlord's land price is, let's not discuss it for the time being. It's like I buy something and want to sell it for 10,000 yuan. If the other party doesn't want it, they can simply not buy it. How can they renege after buying it? It is found that only the plaintiffs and five others in Chengzhi Lane are opposing, and the other tenants have no objections. Why don't the plaintiffs compare with the people in the same lane, but instead compare with the houses in other places? Moreover, the plaintiffs have not paid rent since filing the lawsuit and have not deposited the rent in the bank. The request for a review is without reason and should be rejected. Judge Zhu Cheng issued an order to postpone the hearing for further review.

Sequel to the Deng Yulin Hit-and-Run Case 188

Such Wrongful Souls are Not Easily Dissipated

Deng Yulin, the bursar of Tongwen College on Hongqiao Road in the Shanghai West District, was suddenly hit and killed by a truck transporting bricks and tiles in front of Weile Garden on Haig Road at around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday. The news was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the deceased was 36 years old and lived at No. 20, Lane 289, Hongqiao Road. His father died early, and his mother, Luo, is nearly seventy years old. His wife, Li, is 30 years old and has one son and one daughter. The son's name is Miaogen, who is still in infancy, and the daughter's name is Miaoying, who is only five years old. The family of four relies entirely on Deng for their livelihood, and the family is very poor. Now, unfortunately, he died in an accident, and the whole family is overwhelmed with grief. According to Lao Zhang, a small worker from Gaoyou who witnessed the incident, the deceased's head, face, chest, arms, and other places were all bluish-purple, which proved that he died of suffocation after being injured. The police have ordered the deceased's nephew, Deng Mingxiang, to prepare a coffin for burial and are not investigating the truck that caused the accident, which is difficult to accept. They now plan to petition the court for a re-examination and appeal to all parties to help redress the injustice.

Xu Yan's Dereliction of Duty Case Adjudicated 189

Sentenced to Five Years of Imprisonment

The case of Xu Yan, the captain of the water patrol team, for dereliction of duty, was heard by Judge Shen yesterday morning. Xu and Zhang Xiaogou, who posted and wrote the Jiang Shihe receipts for small goods, were brought to court. Xu Yan was sentenced to five years of imprisonment for one of the three cases against him that were found to be true. Jiang Shihe was sentenced to three years of imprisonment, and Zhang Xiaohe was sentenced to ten months of imprisonment. Xu was not satisfied with the judgment, and the judge ordered that an appeal could be filed within the legal deadline. He was then taken back into custody.

Good News for the Development of National Products 190

In the midst of the appreciation of gold and the depreciation of silver, the value of imported goods is very high and the supply is gradually decreasing. Therefore, those who previously sold foreign goods now have no choice but to sell national products to maintain the market. It is now learned that the various goods produced by the Paris Cosmetics Factory in Shanghai are not only welcomed by the citizens of Shanghai, but especially by the large number of merchants from other provinces. For example, the stores in Tianjin, Hankou, Chongqing, and Guangzhou are all ordering various goods from the factory to be shipped and sold. This is truly good news for the development of national products and a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. It is hoped that the major manufacturers in Shanghai will work hard to manufacture and improve their products, so that the sales of national products will not be inferior to the exclusive beauty of the Paris Cosmetics Factory.

Soochow University Holds National Music Concert 191

Yangshu. Since its establishment, the Soochow University National Music Society has been making steady progress due to the guidance of Wu. In order to thoroughly promote and improve the national music movement, the society will hold a concert at the school's auditorium on the 16th of this month and at the YMCA on Sichuan Road on the 17th. The program is very rich. In addition to the society's members performing Maple Bridge Night Mooring, which was composed by the local pipa expert Zhu Xingqing, and the polyphonic four-part Cantonese music, which was composed by the music expert Wu Bochao, they have also hired Gao Ji, a top student from the National Academy of Music, and national music experts from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to perform and sing. The results will be considerable at that time. It is said that the society is also scheduled to perform in Suzhou on the 23rd.

The History of the Revolution Before the Founding of the Republic is Selling Well 192

The History of the Revolution Before the Founding of the Republic of China was written by Feng Junziyou, a revolutionary pioneer. The entire text contains more than 600,000 words, with more than 200 inserted image plates. It records in detail all the uprisings, assassinations, fundraising, publicity, and various movements from Sun Yat-sen's founding of the Xingzhonghui in the year of Yìwèi until the Wuchang Uprising in the year of Xinhai. It is truly the most abundant and complete masterpiece since the history of the Republic of China. The first volume was published not long ago and became popular for a time. Now the second volume has also been published, and the records of the various revolutionary battles described are mostly the author's participation in the work, so it is even more detailed than the first volume. It is said that the third volume will also be published soon. Recently, the Revolutionary History Editorial Office believes that all members of the National Assembly should be full of common sense about the revolution and the establishment of the country. Therefore, they have sent letters to the representatives of the National Assembly, stating that if they directly purchase the History of the Revolution from the editorial office, they will be given a 50% discount to express their welcome.

Various Labor Union News 193

Dongjiadu Boat Workers' Union: Yesterday, the executive committee meeting was held, chaired by Zhao Shunxiang (A). He reported that the Yitaixing ship had collided with four boats at the pier, and after zealous negotiations by Zhao Shunxiang and Zhao Jinfa on behalf of the union, a satisfactory result was achieved with compensation of sixty-eight yuan. (B) Discussion: (1) Regarding the previous letter to the Third District, Third Precinct Public Security Bureau, advising all sectors to unload heavy goods along the near shore to avoid damaging the docks, but after many days, the situation remained unchanged. It was resolved to send another letter to the Third District, Third Precinct to issue a notice to advise and order compliance. (2) Recently, it was found that non-members were working at the pier. It was resolved to issue a notice advising them to join the union. Those who do not comply should be suspended from work. The meeting adjourned.

Lead Printing Industry Union: Yesterday, the seventh joint meeting of directors and supervisors was held, chaired by Qu Shou Kang. The ceremony was conducted as usual. (1) Chairman's report, "Omitted for brevity." (2) Yao Suikai reported that on May 11th, the newspaper reported that the Municipal Training Association had issued reorganization preparation fees to various labor unions, including the Lead Printing Industry Union of the Third Special District. After the brothers inquired with the Municipal Party Headquarters, it was said that it was a misprint. (3) Comrade Xia Hailin reported on the progress of the union's work. (4) Liang Ling reported on the economic situation of the preparations to date. (5) Qu Shou Kang proposed to invite Chen Zuwang as a volunteer assistant to the union's organization department, which was approved. (6) Yao Suikai proposed that Gu Jingen, a worker in this city, was shot and killed by imperialists for no reason. It was resolved to issue a declaration and Yao Suikai was publicly elected to be responsible for drafting it. (7) Yao Suikai proposed that responsible personnel in various departments of the union often fail to attend meetings. It was resolved to first write a letter to advise them. (8) Omitted. (9) The union's director and supervisor badges have already been made. Those who have not yet received them should come to the union to collect them. It was resolved and the meeting adjourned.

Shanghai South District Cotton Weaving Industry Union: Yesterday, a standing committee meeting of the directors was held, chaired by Zhou Xuebo. A. Chairman's report, omitted. B. Discussion and resolutions: (1) Jinxin Factory dismissed Huang Agou and four others for no reason. The issue has not been resolved for a long time. How to negotiate? It was resolved to submit a request to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, requesting prompt handling. (2) Thirty-five and thirty-two female workers at Sanxin Factory fought each other and were dismissed by the factory. The union sent personnel to negotiate with the factory, requesting reinstatement. The factory manager agreed to investigate, but the work has not been restored for a long time. How should this be handled? It was resolved to send a letter from the union to inquire with the factory manager. (3) Ni Tingzai proposed that the union should appoint a standing director to be responsible for carrying out union affairs. It was resolved to elect Zhou Yuebo as the standing director of the union. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Weather Report 194

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that mist was gradually appearing in the Yangtze River basin and the coastal area south of Ma'an Island. The southeast wind was quite strong here. The wind along the Shandong coast varied from southwest to northwest. Also, at 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the port in the past 24 hours was 72.5 and the lowest was 50.4. On the same day last year, the highest was 75.0 and the lowest was 62.1.

Letter 195

Dear Editor, Regarding the "Municipal Chamber of Commerce Petition for Relief of Difficulties in Various Industries" published in today's edition of your newspaper, the matters concerning our industry are tantamount to fundamentally eliminating our industry. Please note that "譜" is actually a typo for "爆" [explosives]. Also, "買" [buy] in "取消硝磺買賣制" [abolish the buying and selling system of saltpeter and sulfur] is actually a typo for "公" [public]. This special letter is to request a correction. Sincerely, To the Chief Editor, Shanghai Explosives Industry Trade Association, May 13th.

Youth Garden

Elder Sister 196

— Weinan

...A small memento...

"Elder Sister, you stand in the middle, okay?"

"Yes, the oldest sister should be in the middle."

This was one day during summer vacation last year. At that time, Zhi and I lived together in a pavilion house in Xieqiao, living our small family-style life. We made the usual trip to the hospital every day, and spent the rest of our time in that small room. The two of us worked together for more than a month and felt much healthier and fatter than when we were at school.

Under this strong sunlight, we became familiar with the owner of the ice cream shop. In the evening, wearing slippers and holding a fan, we would go over to his place. After another ten days or so, we felt too bored. As a result, we made friends with watermelon for a few days to relieve our summer heat.

Zhi fell ill. Zhi really fell on the bed and couldn't go with me. This was my responsibility. Was ice cream and watermelon delicious?... After blaming myself for a while, I urged Zhi to seek treatment.

The two of us, who often gathered in one place, were as close as siblings. Moreover, Zhi was a guest here with no relatives to depend on. I felt sad for this poor person. The illness became more serious day by day. My personal ability was limited. Zhi later understood my difficulties and invited my good friend Qing from Hangzhou to Shanghai.

Qing was more experienced. She said that going to the hospital would be easier. Zhi reluctantly agreed. At this time, I felt like a bird out of a cage, much more relaxed.

Living in the hospital was so happy. The patient gradually recovered. Qing and I gradually became close to each other. Mr. Zhang once said that we were a trinity. We had already silently acknowledged it in our hearts.

Just as we were setting up our belongings in Ward No. 5 where Zhi was staying... The supplies from the residence in Xieqiao were gradually moved to the hospital... Unexpectedly, we had to leave it again. I was a little reluctant, but wouldn't it be too uneconomical to not live there when the illness was cured?

There was still a week before the start of school. Qing was about to return to Hangzhou. I suggested that the three of us take a photo together as a memento of Zhi's nursing during her illness and as a farewell to Qing leaving Shanghai. The three of us agreed and rushed to take it. At that time, the tram was on strike. Let's take a rickshaw, we got the consent.

I, who was the youngest but had to be someone else's elder sister, liked people calling me elder sister the most. Zhi and Qing both understood this and affectionately called me elder sister. I was happy. Having these two good younger sisters standing on both sides increased the blessings of the old elder sister.

Gatherings and separations are impermanent, and human affairs are ever-changing. This is really true. I haven't seen Qing for a long time. Zhi has returned to her hometown again. As for me, although I am still living a school life, the atmosphere at school has been extremely tense recently. The problem of registration. If we don't work hard and can't achieve our goal, I will have to leave these old friends and beloved Shanghai. Qing, Zhi, I miss you. Looking forward to your good news from afar, I wrote these manuscripts recalling old things in front of our group photo. Can you see them? Can you remember your old elder sister at the same time?
